
You are a premier expert in software testing, specializing in solving fuzzing compilation and build issues. These problems are often caused by mismatches between fuzzing configuration files and the project's source files. I will provide you with error logs from the oss-fuzz build process for different projects. Based on the error messages, configuration files, and other information, you are to provide targeted solutions. Strive to avoid altering files unrelated to the problem, with the ultimate goal of enabling the project to compile and build successfully.
Next, the Dockerfile, build.sh, project.yaml, file tree, and error log for mosquitto will be provided. Please read and analyze the file tree and the given information, identify which files might be causing the problem‚Äîwhether they are core fuzz testing build files like Dockerfile and build.sh, or files within the mosquitto project itself‚Äîand attempt to propose a solution.

FROM gcr.io/oss-fuzz-base/base-builder

# Add cache-busting layer to ensure fresh clone
ARG CACHE_BUST=1

# Main repo
RUN git clone --depth 1 -b develop https://github.com/eclipse/mosquitto ${SRC}/mosquitto

# Apply fixes for protoc path and dependency installation
RUN sed -i 's|PROTOC?=/src/libprotobuf-mutator/external.protobuf/bin/protoc|PROTOC?=\${SRC}/LPM/external.protobuf/bin/protoc|' ${SRC}/mosquitto/fuzzing/libcommon/Makefile && \
    sed -i '/# If building outside of oss-fuzz, we need LPM/,/^fi$/c\\# If building outside of oss-fuzz, we need LPM\\n# Check if protoc is available, build LPM if not\\nif [ ! -f \${SRC}/LPM/external.protobuf/bin/protoc ]; then\\n\\t# Clone libprotobuf-mutator if not already present\\n\\tif [ ! -d \${SRC}/libprotobuf-mutator ]; then\\n\\t\\tgit clone https://github.com/google/libprotobuf-mutator \${SRC}/libprotobuf-mutator\\n\\tfi\\n\\t\\n\\t# Build LPM\\n\\tmkdir -p \${SRC}/LPM \\\\n\\t\\t\\&\\& cd \${SRC}/LPM \\\\n\\t\\t\\&\\& cmake ../libprotobuf-mutator -GNinja -DLIB_PROTO_MUTATOR_DOWNLOAD_PROTOBUF=ON -DLIB_PROTO_MUTATOR_TESTING=OFF -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release \\\\n\\t\\t\\&\\& ninja\\nfi' ${SRC}/mosquitto/fuzzing/scripts/oss-fuzz-dependencies.sh

# Get dependencies
RUN $SRC/mosquitto/fuzzing/scripts/oss-fuzz-dependencies.sh

WORKDIR $SRC/mosquitto
COPY build.sh $SRC/
